'jig rten gyi chos dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos dang / zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos dang / zag pa zad pa'i chos dang / 'dus byas kyi chos dang / 'dus ma byas kyi chos dang / gnyis su med pa'i chos rnams te/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos rnam pa bcu po 'di la dad cing gus par byed pa dang / ji skad thos pa rnams ci nus su gzungs su 'dzin cing yid la byed do// rab tu rtog go// mthar khong du chud par byed cing gzhan dag la yang ci rigs par ston par byed do// nam chos ston pa'i tshe na phrag dog med pa'i sems dang / ser sna med pa'i sems dang / nga rgyal med pa'i sems dang / rnyed par mi re ba'i sems dang / gzhan mi smod pa'i sems dang / bdag mi stod pa'i sems dang / bsti stang dang bcas pa'i sems dang / phan pa'i sems dang / byams pa chen po'i sems dang / snying rje chen po'i sems su bya'o// nyan thos kyi theg pa can gyi gang zag la ni nyan thos kyi chos ston cing 'chad kyi/ de la rang sangs rgyas kyi chos sam/ theg pa chen po'i chos kyis ma yin pa dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa can gyi gang zag la ni rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'i chos ston gyi/ nyan thos kyi theg pa'i chos sam/ theg pa chen po'i chos kyis ma yin pa dang / theg pa chen po'i gang zag la ni theg pa chen po'i chos ston gyi/ nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa pa'i chos kyis ma yin pa dang / sems can gyi dbang po dang / snod ji lta ba bzhin du dam pa'i chos ston gyi/ dbang po dang snod du ma gyur pa la chos mi ston to// gang theg pa chen po'i sems can la rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa spyod cig par ram/ nyan thos kyi theg pa spyod cig par mi skul lo// rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa can gyi sems can la skabs kha cig tu theg pa chen po'i spyod pa la nan tan byos shig ces skul ba'i skabs ni yod de/ nyan thos kyi theg pa can gyi sems can la skabs kha cig tu rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'i spyod pa dang / theg pa chen po'i spyod pa la nan tan gyis shig ces skul ba'i skabs kyang yod de/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa'i dam pa'i chos chung ngu na tshigs su bcad pa gcig gam tshigs su bcad pa phyed tsam la yang shin tu dad cing bkur sti byed kyi/ de la 'phya ba'am skur pa'am/ bgegs sam/ bar chad mi byed de/ chos ston pa la sangs rgyas dang 'dra bar 'du shes pa dang / chos nyan pa'i 'khor rnams la nad pa dang 'dra bar 'du shes pa dang / gang 'chad pa'i chos la sman bzang po dang 'dra bar 'du shes shing 'dod pa rnam pa lnga yongs su bcad de re ba med pas dam pa'i chos ston to// rigs kyi bu 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i chos kyi sbyin pa'i go cha chen po'i 'khor lo rnam pa bcu zhes bya'o// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang 'khor lo de dang ldan na 'dod pa lnga yongs su bsal te/ myur du nyi ma'i sgron ma'i 'od ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin thob cing nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad las shin tu 'das pa dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing du 'gyur ba dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa pa thams cad kyis mchod pa dang / bsrung ba dang / bsnyen bkur byed par 'gyur ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis don 'di dag gsal bar bzlas pa'i phyir tshigs su bcad de bka' stsal pa/ mkhas pa chos kyi sbyin pa spyod pa dag // snod bzhin theg pa gsum gyi chos ston to// theg pa gzhan dag de la ston mi byed// thos nas de la 'phya zhing skur mi 'gyur// dbang po snod bzhin dam pa'i chos ston gyi// dbang po snod min dag la ma yin no// so sor ji ltar ci la mos pa bzhin// de dang de yi chos ston mgu bar byed// theg pa chen po spyod pa'i gang zag la// theg pa rnam pa gnyis kyi chos mi bstan// bar rab theg pa gnyis kyi gang zag la// theg pa 'bring dang rab kyi chos ston to// shin tu dad cing gus pas chos mnyan gyi// de la 'phya zhing skur bar mi bya'o// chos smra ba la mchod pa byed pa ni// sangs rgyas 'dra bar de la 'du shes bskyed// kun nas nyon mongs pa yi nad bsal phyir// dam pa'i chos kyi sman dag nyan par bskul// khe dang grags pa shin tu ring spangs te// dam pa'i chos dag bstan cing bshad par bya// rigs kyi bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i tshul rang sangs rgyas thams cad las shin tu 'das pa/ nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing chen por 'gyur ba dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa pa thams cad kyis mchod pa dang / bsrung ba dang / bsnyen bkur bya bar 'gyur ro// de la ji ltar na tshul khrims rnam par dag pa go cha chen po'i 'khor lo zhe na/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims rnam par dag pa rnam pa gnyis te/ thun mong ba dang / thun mong ba ma yin no// de la ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims rnam par dag pa'i 'khor lo thun mong ba zhe na/ gang khyim na gnas pa dge bsnyen pha dang / dge bsnyen ma'i tshul khrims kyi sdom pa blangs pa'am/ yang na rab tu byung ba so sor thar pa'i tshul khrims kyis bsnyen par rdzogs pa ste/ sdom pa 'di dang so sor thar pa'i tshul khrims 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims rnam par dag pa'i 'khor lo thun mong ba ste/ nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad dang thun mong ba yin no// byang chub sems dpa' tshul khrims kyi 'khor lo rnam par dag pa 'di'i dbang gis sems can thams cad kyi kun nas nyon mongs pa chod par ram/ log par lta ba sel bar ram/ las kyi sgrib pa dang / 'khor ba las grol bar mi 'gyur te/ go cha chen po'i 'khor lo zhes kyang mi bya/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po zhes kyang mi bya ste/ nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing yang dag pa ma yin no// de la ji ltar na/ byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims rnam par dag pa go cha chen po'i 'khor lo thun mong ma yin pa zhe na/ gang byang chub sems dpa' rnams phyogs bcu'i sems can thams cad la mnyam pa nyid kyi sems dang / gnod pa med pa'i sems dang / khon du 'dzin pa med pa'i sems kyis rnam par dag pa'i tshul khrims srung ngo // tshul khrims dang / tshul khrims ngan pa can dang / sbyin pa dang / ser sna dang / byams pa dang / zhe sdang dang / brtson 'grus dang / le lo can rab 'bring tha ma kun la bye brag mi 'byed pa'i sems dang / khyad par med pa'i 'du shes kyis tshul khrims yongs su srung ngo // khams gsum gyi sems can thams cad la zhe sdang med pa dang / khong khro ba med pa dang / ngan par spyod pa med pas tshul khrims yongs su srung ngo // srid pa gsum gyi phung po dang / khams dang / skye mched la rnam par rtog pa med pas tshul khrims yongs su srung ngo // 'dod pa'i khams la mi gnas par tshul khrims srung ngo // gzugs yod pa'i khams la mi gnas par tshul khrims srung ngo // gzugs med pa'i khams la mi gnas par tshul khrims srung ngo // srid pa'i rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu thams cad la mi gnas par tshul khrims srung ngo // rnyed pa dang mi rnyed pa la mi gnas par tshul khrims srung ngo // 'du byed rnams la mi gnas par tshul khrims srung ste/ 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims rnam par dag pa go cha chen po'i 'khor lo thun mong ma yin pa zhes bya'o// rigs kyi bu byang ba'i sems dang / tshad med pa'i sems dang / phung po dang / khams dang / skye mched thams cad la mngon par 'du mi byed pa'i sems kyis gang nas gang du skyes kyang g.yo ba med pa dang / mi gnas pa'i // nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing du 'gyur ba dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa pa thams cad kyis mchod pa dang / srung ba dang / bsnyen bkur tu dpag dka' nam mkha' 'dra ste// gnas pa med de gzugs kyang med do// byang chub sems dpa'i brtson 'grus chen po// yon tan chen po dang ni ldan te// rgyal ba'i ye shes snying rje chen pos// dpa' bo 'jig rten 'da' bar des 'gyur// mgon dang skyabs med sems can dag ni// 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal rnyog pas bcings pa// snying rje chen po'i chu yis bkrus te// sems can rnam par grol bar byed do// byang can// ngan song dag tu ltung bar 'gyur ba// snying rje chen po'i chu yis bkrus te// sdug bsngal kun las grol bar byed do// rigs kyi bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po tshig so so yang dag par rig pa/ nam mkha'i dbyings dang mnyam pa/ tshad med pa/ mtha' yas pa/ shin tu rgya chen po dang ldan pa ji snyed sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad de/ ting nge 'dzin rnams dang / gzungs du/ sems mnyam pa nyid du gyur pa/ mtshan ma med pa rten pa med pa mi gnas pa/ gos pa med pa'i ting nge 'dzin thams cad kyi sgo dang / gzungs kyi sgo thams cad la sems kyi spyod pa med pa/ mig dang / spyod pa dang / rtag tu sangs rgyas mthong ba dang mi 'bral ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang / nyan thos kyi nye gnas mthong ba dang mi 'bral ba dang / chos thos pa dang mi 'bral ba dang / dge 'dun chung ngu na rmi lam du yang bar chad med par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu de la ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po tshig so so yang dag par rig pas nam mkha'i dbyings dang mnyam pa/ tshad med pa/ mtha' yas pa/ yangs shing rgya che ba dang ldan pas ji snyed sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad de/ ting nge 'dzin rnams dang / gzungs rnams dang / shin tu brtan pa'i bzod pa'i go cha chen po'i 'khor lo 'dren par 'gyur zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams bsam gtan dang po nas bsam gtan bzhi pa'i bar du snyoms par 'jug pa dang / nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched nas 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched kyi bar du snyoms par 'jug pa dang / 'du shes dang tshor ba 'gog pa'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par 'jug pa'i ting nge 'dzin 'di la gnas na tshor ba rnam gsum dang / 'du byed gsum po yongs su bcad de/ mngon par 'du byed pa dang / g.yo ba'i sems kyi spyod pa med pa/ tshor ba dang / 'du shes dang / sems pa dang / rig pa dang / yid la byed pa la sogs pa kun gcod par 'gyur ro// ting nge 'dzin 'di la gnas na zhag gcig gam/ zhag bdun gyi bar du bsam gtan gyi zas za bar 'gyur ro// ting nge 'dzin de las langs na yang sems rab tu zhi ba len pa med cing // lhan ner gnas par 'gyur ro// gzhan yang don dam pa'i mthas gtugs pa'i stong pa nyid kyi ting nge 'dzin la mnyam par 'jog go// ting nge 'dzin de la gnas na sems rab tu mnyam pas nam mkha' ltar chags pa med pa dang / lus kyi ba spu'i bu ga kun nas zil dngar gyi thigs pa skar ma lta bu/ mngon par byung bas kun nas nyon mongs pas bcings pa'i yongs su gdung ba thams cad sel bar 'gyur ro// ting nge 'dzin de las langs nas yang dag pa'i dran pa thob ste/ dga' ba khyad par can gyis lus la khyab par gyur pa ni ji ltar lha'i sras po dang / dbang phyug chen po dang / bde ba'i ting nge 'dzin thams cad la 'jug pa nas lus kyi ba spu'i khung bu kun nas rab tu bde ba myong ba bzhin de ltar byang chub sems dpa' de lus la bde bas reg pas sangs rgyas rjes su dran par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas rjes su dran pas sangs rgyas mthong ba las mtshan ma gzhan mthong ba med do// byang chub sems dpa' de'i tshe sangs rgyas gcig yid la byas na sangs rgyas gcig mthong ngo // gal te sangs rgyas mang po yid la byas na sangs rgyas mang po mthong ngo // gal te sangs rgyas kyi sku chung bar yid la byas na sangs rgyas kyi sku chung ngur mthong ngo // gal te sangs rgyas kyi sku chen por yid la byas na sangs rgyas kyi sku chen por mthong ngo // gal te sangs rgyas kyi sku tshad med par yid la byas na sangs rgyas kyi sku tshad med par mthong ngo // gal te bdag gi lus sangs rgyas kyi sku'i mtshan dang ldan par yid la byas na bdag gi lus de sangs rgyas kyi sku dang 'dra bar mtshan phun sum tshogs par mthong ngo // gal te gzhan gyi lus sangs rgyas kyi skur yid la byas na gzhan gyi lus sangs rgyas kyi sku dang 'dra bar mtshan phun sum tshogs par mthong ngo // gal te sems can dang sems can ma yin pa dang / ji snyed gzugs su gtogs pa thams cad sangs rgyas kyi sku mtshan dang ldan par yid la byas na sems can dang / sems can ma yin pa dang / ji snyed gzugs su gtogs pa thams cad sangs rgyas kyi sku dang 'dra bar mtshan phun sum tshogs par mthong gi gzugs gzhan du mi mthong ngo // byang chub sems dpa' de'i tshe yang 'di snyam du chos thams cad dang / gzugs thams cad ni sgyu ma dang 'dra ste/ yang dag pa ma yin pas bdag gis tshor ba rnam gsum dang / 'du byed gsum la sogs pa chos thams cad lhag ma ma lus par yongs su gcad do snyam nas 'gog pa'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so// ting nge 'dzin de la gnas nas blo sngon du btang ba bzhin du thams cad yongs su bcad de ting nge 'dzin gyi ro'i zas kyis 'tsho'o// gal te na zhag bdun nam/ zhag bdun gnyis sam/ bdun gsum mam/ bzhi'am/ lnga'am/ drug gam/ bdun nam/ brgyad dam/ gal te na bskal pa tshad med pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong gi bar du ci nus su gnas te/ ting nge 'dzin gyi zas za'o// ting nge 'dzin de las langs nas sems rab tu zhi bas ci la yang mi chags te bde bar gnas so// gal te don dam pa'i mthas gtugs pa'i ting nge 'dzin la zhugs na yang sngar ji skad bshad pa bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi sku mtshan dang ldan pa yid la bya ba nas chos thams cad dang / gzugs thams cad sgyu ma dang 'dra ste yang dag pa ma yin pa'i bar du chud par byed do// rigs kyi bu myur du skye// mngon par 'tshang rgya byang chub chen po 'thob// sangs rgyas mtshan dang ldan pa'i sems can dag // sangs rgyas zhing der yongs su gang bar 'gyur// thams cad sangs rgyas theg la 'dun pa ste// nyan thos rang rgyal theg pa yongs su spong // 'phags pa shin tu rgyas pa chen po sa'i snying po'i 'khor lo bcu pa bya ba las bsod nams kyi zhing gi mtshan nyid kyi le'u zhes bya ste bdun pa'o// // bcom ldan 'das kyis theg pa chen po'i rnam grangs 'di bshad pa'i tshe 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor de'i nang na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed dang mnyam pa sngon 'das pa'i dus na sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa la goms pa dag deng 'dir bcom ldan 'das kyis sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa la nan tan bya ba'i sbyor ba bshad pa thos nas sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo mo thams cad thob bo// gzhan yang sems can tshad med grangs med pa rnams chos 'di thos nas ting nge 'dzin gyi 'tsho ba me tog gi phreng ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi sgo mo thams cad thob bo// gzhan yang sems can tshad med grangs med pa dag bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad pa thos nas dpa' bar 'gro ba glog gi 'od la rten pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi sgo mo thams cad thob bo// gzhan yang sems can tshad med grangs med pa dag bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad pa thos nas chos la sgyur ba 'od snang ba las rten par byed pa rjes su 'thun pa'i bzod pa thams cad thob bo// gzhan yang sems can tshad med grangs med pa dag bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad pa thos nas rdul dang dri ma dang bral te chos la chos kyi mig rnam par dag pa skyes te rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu thob bo// gzhan yang sems can tshad med grangs med pa dag ni bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad pa thos nas lan cig phyir ldog pa'i 'bras bu thob bo// gzhan yang sems can tshad med grangs med pa dag bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad pa thos nas phyir mi ldog pa'i 'bras bu thob bo// gzhan yang sems can tshad med grangs med pa dag bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad pa thos nas mchog gi dgra bcom pa'i 'bras bu thob bo// gzhan yang sems can tshad med grangs med pa dag bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad pa thos nas khams gsum gyi btson ra nas 'byung bar rtsom pas bcom ldan 'das la rten cing rab tu byung nas yang dag pa'i chos la zhugs par gyur to// gzhan yang sems can tshad med grangs med pa dag na ma 'tsho'i bar du dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam la bde bar gnas shing nyan thos kyi theg par sems bskyed pas phyir mi ldog par gyur to// gzhan yang sems can tshad med grangs med pa dag bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad pa thos nas nam 'tsho'i bar du dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam la bde bar gnas nas/ rang sangs rgyas kyi theg par sems bskyed pa las phyir mi ldog par gyur to// gzhan yang sems can tshad med grangs med pa dag bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad pa thos nas nam 'tsho'i bar du dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam la bde bar gnas nas theg pa chen por sems bskyed cing bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par gyur to// gzhan yang sems can tshad med grangs med pa dag ni bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad pa thos nas 'jig rten gyi yang dag par lta ba thob par gyur te/ yang dag par lta ba de'i dbang gis ngan song du 'gro ba'i rgyu dang / kun nas nyon mongs pa'i las dang / nyon mongs pa thams cad byang nas mtho ris su 'gro ba'i rgyu dang / yang dag pa'i smon lam dang / dge ba'i las thams cad skye zhing 'phel bar 'gyur ro// gzhan yang sems can tshad med grangs med pa dag bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad pa thos nas dkon mchog gsum la skyabs su song ste/ dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa blangs nas sangs rgyas mchod pa la spro ba dang / chos thos pa la dga' ba dang / dge 'dun gyi g.yog byed pa la mos te/ nyin mtshan du 'bad pa'i brtson 'grus la sems par tshad med par gyur to// gzhan yang sems can tshad med grangs med pa dag bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad pa thos nas log pa la 'bab pa dang / log pa la phyogs pa dang / blo gros ngan pa dang / las ngan pa thams cad yongs su spangs te/ sangs rgyas kyi chos la mi 'gyur ba'i dad pa thob nas khyim na gnas pa'i chos yongs su spangs te rnam par dag pas rab tu byung bar gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po nam mkha'i snying po la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu ngas sa'i snying po'i 'khor lo bcu pa zhes bya ba brda sprod pa chen po chos kyi sgo mo 'di/ khyod kyi lag tu gtad kyis khyod kyis gzungs su zung la shin tu rgyas par gyis shig // sems can gang chos kyi rnam grangs 'di la klog gam/ 'don tam/ yid la byed dam/ gzhan la yang rgya cher 'chad dam/ yang dag pa'i spyad pa la gnas pa dag la khyod kyis chos rnam pa 'di bcus bsrungs te/ yun ring por phan pa dang bde ba'i don thob par gyis shig // bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ de'i thabs dang bdog pa'i nor thams cad bsrungs te nyams par mi bya ba dang / gnod pa thams cad las bsrungs te/ gnod pa med par bya ba dang / log par lta ba dang / log par phyogs pa las bsrungs te mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam spang bar bya ba dang / de'i lus dang ngag la gnod pa thams cad las bsrungs te med par bya ba dang / 'phya ba dang skur pa thams cad las bsrungs te med par bya ba dang / tshul khrims dang spyod pa thams cad nyams par mi 'gyur bar srung ba dang / de la mi ma yin pa thams cad dang / 'byung ba chen po 'khrugs pa dang / dus ma yin pa'i nad dang / mi dge ba thams cad yongs su sel bar srung ba dang / de la dus ma yin pa tshul ma yin pa/ ltas ngan dang / rims thams cad mi 'byung bar srung ba dang / de la 'chi ba'i dus byed pa na yang sangs rgyas thams cad mthong bar srung ba dang / de tshe 'phos nas kyang bde 'gror skye ba dang / phan pa dang bde ba'i don thob par yongs su srung bar byed do// rigs kyi bu sems can gang chos kyi rnam grangs 'di klog pa dang / 'don pa dang / don yid la byed pa dang / gzhan la rgya cher 'chad dam/ yang dag pa'i spyod pa la gnas pa dag la khyod kyis chos rnam pa 'di bcus shin tu bsrungs shing // byin gyis brlabs te/ chos rnam pa 'di bcus yun ring por phan pa dang bde bar gyis shig // de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po nam mkha'i snying pos bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// de de bzhin no// bcom ldan 'das bdag gis chos kyi rnam grangs gzungs su 'dzin cing shin tu rgyas par bgyi'o// sems can gang chos kyi rnam grangs 'di la klog pa dang / 'don pa dang / don yid la bgyid pa dang / pha rol po la rgya cher ston pa dang / yang dag pa'i spyod pa la gnas pa dag la bdag gis chos rnam pa 'di bcus shin tu bsrungs te yun ring por phan pa dang bde bar bgyi'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis mdo sde 'di gsungs nas/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor de na gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po nam mkha'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rigs par the tsom 'dri ba dang / tshangs pa chen po lha'i snying po dang / lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa la sogs pa 'khor mang po thams cad bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par dga'o// // 'dus pa chen po las byang chub sems dpa' sa'i snying po'i 'khor lo bcu pa las bde ba'i don thob pa yongs su gdams pa zhes bya ba'i le'u ste brgyad do// // 'dus pa chen po byang chub sems dpa' sa'i snying po'i 'khor lo bcu pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo rdzogs so// // rgya'i mkhan po hwa shang zab mo la sogs pa dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsa ba ban de rnam par mi rtog gis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
